authentication is implemented through a sophisticated layered architecture:\\n\\n## Main Orchestrator: SaslChannelBuilder\\nThe `SaslChannelBuilder` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/SaslChannelBuilder.java) serves as the primary orchestrator for SASL authentication on the broker side. When building a server channel, it:\\n1. Creates mechanism-specific callback handlers via `createServerCallbackHandlers()` which selects the appropriate handler based on the configured SASL mechanism\\n2. Instantiates the main broker-side authenticator via `buildServerAuthenticator()`\\n3. Manages JAAS contexts and credential caches for each mechanism\\n\\n## Core Authenticator: SaslServerAuthenticator\\nThe `SaslServerAuthenticator` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerAuthenticator.java) is the main broker-side SASL authenticator implementing a state machine with states like INITIAL_REQUEST, HANDSHAKE_REQUEST, AUTHENTICATE, COMPLETE, FAILED, and support for re-authentication. It:\\n1. Manages the SASL handshake protocol (SaslHandshakeRequest/Response)\\n2. Processes SaslAuthenticateRequest/Response messages\\n3. Creates mechanism-specific SaslServer instances via `createSaslServer()` method\\n4. For GSSAPI: Calls `createSaslKerberosServer()` to handle Kerberos authentication\\n5. For other mechanisms (PLAIN, SCRAM, OAUTHBEARER): Uses standard javax.security.sasl.Sasl factory methods\\n\\n## PLAIN Mechanism Implementation\\nPLAIN authentication is implemented by:\\n- `PlainSaslServer` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainSaslServer.java): Implements SaslServer interface with `evaluateResponse()` method that parses PLAIN protocol messages (authzid, authcid, password)\\n- `PlainSaslServerProvider` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainSaslServerProvider.java): Factory for creating PlainSaslServer instances\\n- `PlainServerCallbackHandler` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainServerCallbackHandler.java): Handles credential verification callbacks for PLAIN\\n\\n## SCRAM Mechanism Implementation\\nSCRAM (Salted Challenge Response Authentication Mechanism) authentication is implemented by:\\n- `ScramSaslServer` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramSaslServer.java): Implements SaslServer with complex state machine (RECEIVE_CLIENT_FIRST_MESSAGE, RECEIVE_CLIENT_FINAL_MESSAGE, COMPLETE, FAILED) for SCRAM protocol\\n- `ScramSaslServerProvider` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramSaslServerProvider.java): Factory for creating ScramSaslServer\\n- `ScramServerCallbackHandler` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramServerCallbackHandler.java): Verifies SCRAM credentials from broker's credential cache\\n- `ScramMechanism` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramMechanism.java): Defines SCRAM-SHA-256 and SCRAM-SHA-512 mechanism types\\n- `ScramMessages` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramMessages.java): Defines SCRAM protocol message structures\\n- `ScramFormatter` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramFormatter.java): Formats and parses SCRAM credentials\\n- `ScramCredentialUtils` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramCredentialUtils.java): Utility methods for credential handling\\n\\n## OAuthBearer Mechanism Implementation\\nOAuthBearer token-based authentication is implemented by:\\n- `OAuthBearerSaslServer` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/internals/OAuthBearerSaslServer.java): Implements SaslServer interface for OAuth bearer tokens\\n- `OAuthBearerSaslServerProvider` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/internals/OAuthBearerSaslServerProvider.java): Factory for creating OAuthBearerSaslServer\\n- `OAuthBearerUnsecuredValidatorCallbackHandler` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/internals/unsecured/OAuthBearerUnsecuredValidatorCallbackHandler.java): Validates OAuth bearer tokens\\n\\n## GSSAPI/Kerberos Mechanism Implementation\\nGSSAPI/Kerberos authentication leverages the Java GSSAPI libraries and is configured through:\\n- `KerberosClientCallbackHandler` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/kerberos/KerberosClientCallbackHandler.java): Handles Kerberos callbacks\\n- `KerberosName` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/kerberos/KerberosName.java): Parses and processes Kerberos principal names\\n- `KerberosShortNamer` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/kerberos/KerberosShortNamer.java): Shortens Kerberos principal names using configurable rules\\n- `KerberosLogin` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/kerberos/KerberosLogin.java): Manages Kerberos login\\n- `SaslServerCallbackHandler` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerCallbackHandler.java): Generic server callback handler used as base for Kerberos\\n\\n## Authentication Context and Lifecycle\\nThe authentication context lifecycle is managed through:\\n- `SaslAuthenticationContext` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/SaslAuthenticationContext.java): Encapsulates SASL authentication session information including the SaslServer instance, security protocol, client address, listener name, and optional SSL session\\n- `AuthenticationContext` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/AuthenticationContext.java): Base interface for authentication contexts (also implemented by PlaintextAuthenticationContext and SslAuthenticationContext)\\n- `ReauthenticationContext` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/ReauthenticationContext.java): Manages re-authentication state and lifecycle\\n\\n## Supporting Components\\n- `SaslExtensions` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/SaslExtensions.java) and `SaslExtensionsCallback` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/SaslExtensionsCallback.java): Handle SASL extension negotiations\\n- `AuthenticateCallbackHandler` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/AuthenticateCallbackHandler.java): Base interface for all mechanism-specific callback handlers\\n- `CredentialCache` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/CredentialCache.java): Caches credentials (SCRAM, delegation tokens) by mechanism\\n- `KafkaPrincipalBuilder` and `DefaultKafkaPrincipalBuilder` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/DefaultKafkaPrincipalBuilder.java): Builds Kafka principals from authentication context\\n- `SaslConfigs` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/SaslConfigs.java): Central configuration constants for all SASL mechanisms\\n- `ScramCredential` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/ScramCredential.java) and `ScramCredentialCallback` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/ScramCredentialCallback.java): SCRAM credential structures\\n\\n## Flow Summary\\nThe authentication flow works as follows: 1. Client initiates connection to broker\\n2. SaslChannelBuilder creates SaslServerAuthenticator with all enabled mechanism callback handlers\\n3. Client sends SaslHandshakeRequest with desired mechanism\\n4. SaslServerAuthenticator selects appropriate mechanism and creates mechanism-specific SaslServer via factory (PlainSaslServerProvider, ScramSaslServerProvider, OAuthBearerSaslServerProvider, or Sasl.createSaslServer for standard JDK providers)\\n5. Client and server exchange SASL tokens via SaslAuthenticateRequest/Response\\n6. Mechanism-specific SaslServer.evaluateResponse() validates credentials using corresponding callback handler\\n7. Upon success, SaslAuthenticationContext is created and passed to KafkaPrincipalBuilder to establish the client's identity\\n8. For re-authentication, ReauthenticationContext manages the lifecycle and ensures mechanism consistency\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3337,"cache_read_input_tokens":60351,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3337},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"82eeeeb9-3ab2-4970-948a-e0547aba2c14","uuid":"302d57ff-c05d-49ea-ada2-64cb98b7ebb8"}

(clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/SaslChannelBuilder.java) serves as the primary orchestrator for SASL authentication on the broker side. When building a server channel, it:\\n1. Creates mechanism-specific callback handlers via `createServerCallbackHandlers()` which selects the appropriate handler based on the configured SASL mechanism\\n2. Instantiates the main broker-side authenticator via `buildServerAuthenticator()`\\n3. Manages JAAS contexts and credential caches for each mechanism\\n\\n## Core Authenticator: SaslServerAuthenticator\\nThe `SaslServerAuthenticator` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerAuthenticator.java) is the main broker-side SASL authenticator implementing a state machine with states like INITIAL_REQUEST, HANDSHAKE_REQUEST, AUTHENTICATE, COMPLETE, FAILED, and support for re-authentication. It:\\n1. Manages the SASL handshake protocol (SaslHandshakeRequest/Response)\\n2. Processes SaslAuthenticateRequest/Response messages\\n3. Creates mechanism-specific SaslServer instances via `createSaslServer()` method\\n4. For GSSAPI: Calls `createSaslKerberosServer()` to handle Kerberos authentication\\n5. For other mechanisms (PLAIN, SCRAM, OAUTHBEARER): Uses standard javax.security.sasl.Sasl factory methods\\n\\n## PLAIN Mechanism Implementation\\nPLAIN authentication is implemented by:\\n- `PlainSaslServer` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainSaslServer.java): Implements SaslServer interface with `evaluateResponse()` method that parses PLAIN protocol messages (authzid, authcid, password)\\n- `PlainSaslServerProvider` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainSaslServerProvider.java): Factory for creating PlainSaslServer instances\\n- `PlainServerCallbackHandler` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/plain/internals/PlainServerCallbackHandler.java): Handles credential verification callbacks for PLAIN\\n\\n## SCRAM Mechanism Implementation\\nSCRAM (Salted Challenge Response Authentication Mechanism) authentication is implemented by:\\n- `ScramSaslServer` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramSaslServer.java): Implements SaslServer with complex state machine (RECEIVE_CLIENT_FIRST_MESSAGE, RECEIVE_CLIENT_FINAL_MESSAGE, COMPLETE, FAILED) for SCRAM protocol\\n- `ScramSaslServerProvider` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramSaslServerProvider.java): Factory for creating ScramSaslServer\\n- `ScramServerCallbackHandler` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramServerCallbackHandler.java): Verifies SCRAM credentials from broker's credential cache\\n- `ScramMechanism` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramMechanism.java): Defines SCRAM-SHA-256 and SCRAM-SHA-512 mechanism types\\n- `ScramMessages` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramMessages.java): Defines SCRAM protocol message structures\\n- `ScramFormatter` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramFormatter.java): Formats and parses SCRAM credentials\\n- `ScramCredentialUtils` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramCredentialUtils.java): Utility methods for credential handling\\n\\n## OAuthBearer Mechanism Implementation\\nOAuthBearer Factory for creating OAuthBearerSaslServer\\n- `OAuthBearerUnsecuredValidatorCallbackHandler` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/internals/unsecured/OAuthBearerUnsecuredValidatorCallbackHandler.java): Validates OAuth bearer tokens\\n\\n## GSSAPI/Kerberos Mechanism Implementation\\nGSSAPI/Kerberos authentication leverages the Java GSSAPI libraries and is configured through:\\n- `KerberosClientCallbackHandler` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/kerberos/KerberosClientCallbackHandler.java): Handles Kerberos callbacks\\n- `KerberosName` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/kerberos/KerberosName.java): Parses and processes Kerberos principal names\\n- `KerberosShortNamer` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/kerberos/KerberosShortNamer.java): Shortens Kerberos principal names using configurable rules\\n- `KerberosLogin` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/kerberos/KerberosLogin.java): Manages Kerberos login\\n- `SaslServerCallbackHandler` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerCallbackHandler.java): Generic server callback handler used as base for Kerberos\\n\\n## Authentication Context and Lifecycle\\nThe authentication context lifecycle is managed through:\\n- `SaslAuthenticationContext` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/SaslAuthenticationContext.java): Encapsulates SASL authentication session information including the SaslServer instance, security protocol, client address, listener name, and optional SSL session\\n- `AuthenticationContext` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/auth/AuthenticationContext.java): Base interface for authentication contexts (also implemented by PlaintextAuthenticationContext and SslAuthenticationContext)\\n- `ReauthenticationContext` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/ReauthenticationContext.java): Manages re-authentication state and lifecycle\\n\\n## (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/CredentialCache.java): Caches credentials (SCRAM, delegation tokens) by mechanism\\n- `KafkaPrincipalBuilder` and `DefaultKafkaPrincipalBuilder` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/DefaultKafkaPrincipalBuilder.java): Builds Kafka principals from authentication context\\n- (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/ScramCredential.java) and `ScramCredentialCallback` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/ScramCredentialCallback.java): SCRAM credential structures\\n\\n## Flow Summary\\nThe authentication flow works as follows: 1. Client initiates connection to broker\\n2. SaslChannelBuilder creates SaslServerAuthenticator with all enabled mechanism callback handlers\\n3. Client sends SaslHandshakeRequest with desired mechanism\\n4. SaslServerAuthenticator selects appropriate mechanism and creates mechanism-specific SaslServer via factory (PlainSaslServerProvider, ScramSaslServerProvider, OAuthBearerSaslServerProvider, or Sasl.createSaslServer for standard JDK providers)\\n5. Client and server exchange SASL tokens via SaslAuthenticateRequest/Response\\n6. Mechanism-specific SaslServer.evaluateResponse() validates credentials using corresponding callback handler\\n7. Upon success, SaslAuthenticationContext is created and passed to KafkaPrincipalBuilder to establish the client's identity\\n8. For re-authentication, ReauthenticationContext manages the lifecycle and ensures mechanism consistency\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
